CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS DatabaseVersion (key INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, version INTEGER NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Packages (packageName TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, version INTEGER NOT NULL, params BLOB)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ApplicationStates (packageName TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, version INTEGER NOT NULL, user TEXT NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS MultiCommitApplicationStates (packageName TEXT NOT NULL, version INTEGER NOT NULL, user TEXT NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (packageName, user))
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS LogSources (logSourceID INTEGER NOT NULL, packageName TEXT NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (logSourceID, packageName))
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS LogSourcesIndex ON LogSources (packageName)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Tokens (packageName TEXT NOT NULL, version INTEGER NOT NULL, user TEXT NOT NULL, isCommitted INTEGER NOT NULL, experimentToken BLOB NOT NULL, serverToken TEXT NOT NULL, diffToken TEXT NOT NULL, servingVersion INTEGER DEFAULT 0, PRIMARY KEY (packageName, version, user, isCommitted))
packageName, version, user, isCommitted, experimentToken, serverToken, diffToken, servingVersion
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Flags (packageName TEXT NOT NULL, version INTEGER NOT NULL, user TEXT NOT NULL, partitionID INTEGER NOT NULL, storageType INTEGER NOT NULL, name TEXT NOT NULL, valueType INTEGER NOT NULL, value BLOB, isCommitted INTEGER NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (packageName, version, user, name, isCommitted))
packageName, version, user, partitionId, storageType, name, valueType, value, isCommitted
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS FlagOverrides (packageName TEXT NOT NULL, user TEXT NOT NULL, storageType INTEGER NOT NULL, name TEXT NOT NULL, valueType INTEGER NOT NULL, value BLOB, isCommitted INTEGER NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (packageName, user, name, isCommitted))
packageName, user, storageType, name, valueType, value, isCommitted
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS RequestTags (user TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, bytesTag BLOB NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ChangeCounts (key INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, count INTEGER NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ApplicationTags (packageName TEXT NOT NULL, version INTEGER NOT NULL, user TEXT NOT NULL, partitionID INTEGER NOT NULL, tag BLOB NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (packageName, version, partitionID, user))
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS CrossLoggedExperimentTokens (fromPackage TEXT NOT NULL, fromVersion INTEGER NOT NULL, toPackage TEXT NOT NULL, toVersion INTEGER NOT NULL, user TEXT NOT NULL, provenance INTEGER NOT NULL, isCommitted INTEGER NOT NULL, token BLOB NOT NULL)
fromPackage, fromVersion, toPackage, toVersion, user, provenance, isCommitted, token
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS CrossTokensFromIndex ON CrossLoggedExperimentTokens (fromPackage, fromVersion, isCommitted, user)
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS CrossTokensToIndex ON CrossLoggedExperimentTokens (toPackage, toVersion, isCommitted, user)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS SyncTimes (syncType INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, nextSyncTimeSeconds INTEGER NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS DogfoodsToken (key INTEGER NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, token BLOB NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS SyncedPackages (packageName TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, isFinished INTEGER NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS SyncedPackagesV6 (packageName TEXT NOT NULL, version INTEGER NOT NULL, isFinished INTEGER NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (packageName, isFinished))
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS SyncedUsers (user TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, isFinished INTEGER NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS BundleIDs (packageName TEXT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY, bundleID TEXT NOT NULL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ExternalExperimentIDs (logSourceID INTEGER NOT NULL, namespace TEXT NOT NULL, bundleID TEXT NOT NULL, isBundleScoped INTEGER NOT NULL, experimentIDs BLOB NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (logSourceID, bundleID, namespace, isBundleScoped))
